‚îÇ  38 ‚îÇ                                                             ‚îÇ
‚îÇ  39 ‚îÇ             // Get camera if not assigned                   ‚îÇ
‚îÇ  40 ‚îÇ             if (cameraTransform == null)                    ‚îÇ
‚îÇ  41 ‚îÇ             {                                               ‚îÇ
‚îÇ  42 ‚îÇ                 cameraTransform = Camera.main?.transform;   ‚îÇ
‚îÇ  43 ‚îÇ             }                                               ‚îÇ
‚îÇ  44 ‚îÇ                                                             ‚îÇ
‚îÇ  45 ‚îÇ             // Apply sensitivity from config                ‚îÇ
‚îÇ  46 ‚îÇ             mouseSensitivity = GameConfig.Instance.mouseSensitivity; ‚îÇ
‚îÇ  47 ‚îÇ         }                                                   ‚îÇ
‚îÇ  48 ‚îÇ                                                             ‚îÇ
‚îÇ  49 ‚îÇ         private void Update()                               ‚îÇ
‚îÇ  50 ‚îÇ         {                                                   ‚îÇ
‚îÇ  51 ‚îÇ             HandleGroundCheck();                            ‚îÇ
‚îÇ  52 ‚îÇ             HandleMovement();                               ‚îÇ
‚îÇ  53 ‚îÇ             HandleMouseLook();                              ‚îÇ
‚îÇ  54 ‚îÇ             HandleJumping();                                ‚îÇ
‚îÇ  55 ‚îÇ         }                                                   ‚îÇ
‚îÇ  56 ‚îÇ                                                             ‚îÇ
‚îÇ  57 ‚îÇ         /// <summary>                                       ‚îÇ
‚îÇ  58 ‚îÇ         /// Check if player is grounded                     ‚îÇ
‚îÇ  59 ‚îÇ         /// </summary>                                      ‚îÇ
‚îÇ  60 ‚îÇ         private void HandleGroundCheck()                    ‚îÇ
‚îÇ  61 ‚îÇ         {                                                   ‚îÇ
‚îÇ  62 ‚îÇ             Vector3 spherePosition = transform.position - Vector3.up * controller.height * 0.5f; ‚îÇ
‚îÇ  63 ‚îÇ             isGrounded = Physics.CheckSphere(spherePosition, groundCheckDistance, groundMask); ‚îÇ
‚îÇ  64 ‚îÇ                                                             ‚îÇ
‚îÇ  65 ‚îÇ             if (isGrounded && velocity.y < 0)               ‚îÇ
‚îÇ  66 ‚îÇ             {                                               ‚îÇ
‚îÇ  67 ‚îÇ                 velocity.y = -2f; // Small downward force to keep grounded ‚îÇ
‚îÇ  68 ‚îÇ             }                                               ‚îÇ
‚îÇ  69 ‚îÇ         }                                                   ‚îÇ
‚îÇ  70 ‚îÇ                                                             ‚îÇ
‚îÇ  71 ‚îÇ         /// <summary>                                       ‚îÇ
‚îÇ  72 ‚îÇ         /// Handle player movement input                    ‚îÇ
‚îÇ  73 ‚îÇ         /// </summary>                                      ‚îÇ
‚îÇ  74 ‚îÇ         private void HandleMovement()                       ‚îÇ
‚îÇ  75 ‚îÇ         {                                                   ‚îÇ
‚îÇ  76 ‚îÇ             float horizontal = Input.GetAxis("Horizontal"); ‚îÇ
‚îÇ  77 ‚îÇ             float vertical = Input.GetAxis("Vertical");     ‚îÇ
‚îÇ  78 ‚îÇ                                                             ‚îÇ
‚îÇ  79 ‚îÇ             Vector3 direction = transform.right * horizontal + transform.forward * vertical; ‚îÇ
‚îÇ  80 ‚îÇ             controller.Move(direction * moveSpeed * Time.deltaTime); ‚îÇ
‚îÇ  81 ‚îÇ         }                                                   ‚îÇ
‚îÇ  82 ‚îÇ                                                             ‚îÇ
‚îÇ  83 ‚îÇ         /// <summary>                                       ‚îÇ
‚îÇ  84 ‚îÇ         /// Handle mouse look for camera rotation           ‚îÇ
‚îÇ  85 ‚îÇ         /// </summary>                                      ‚îÇ
‚îÇ  86 ‚îÇ         private void HandleMouseLook()                      ‚îÇ
‚îÇ  87 ‚îÇ         {                                                   ‚îÇ
‚îÇ  88 ‚îÇ             if (cameraTransform == null) return;            ‚îÇ
‚îÇ  89 ‚îÇ                                                             ‚îÇ
‚îÇ  90 ‚îÇ             float mouseX = Input.GetAxis("Mouse X") * mouseSensitivity; ‚îÇ
‚îÇ  91 ‚îÇ             float mouseY = Input.GetAxis("Mouse Y") * mouseSensitivity; ‚îÇ
‚îÇ  92 ‚îÇ                                                             ‚îÇ
‚îÇ  93 ‚îÇ             // Rotate the player body left/right            ‚îÇ
‚îÇ  94 ‚îÇ             transform.Rotate(Vector3.up * mouseX);          ‚îÇ
‚îÇ  95 ‚îÇ                                                             ‚îÇ
‚îÇ  96 ‚îÇ             // Rotate the camera up/down                    ‚îÇ
‚îÇ  97 ‚îÇ             cameraRotationX -= mouseY;                      ‚îÇ
‚îÇ  98 ‚îÇ             cameraRotationX = Mathf.Clamp(cameraRotationX, -maxLookAngle, maxLookAngle); ‚îÇ
‚îÇ  99 ‚îÇ             cameraTransform.localRotation = Quaternion.Euler(cameraRotationX, 0f, 0f); ‚îÇ
‚îÇ 100 ‚îÇ                                                             ‚îÇ
‚îÇ 101 ‚îÇ             // Apply Y-axis inversion if enabled            ‚îÇ
‚îÇ 102 ‚îÇ             if (GameConfig.Instance.invertYAxis)            ‚îÇ
‚îÇ 103 ‚îÇ             {                                               ‚îÇ
‚îÇ 104 ‚îÇ                 cameraRotationX += mouseY * 2; // Reverse the previous subtraction ‚îÇ
‚îÇ 105 ‚îÇ             }                                               ‚îÇ
‚îÇ 106 ‚îÇ         }                                                   ‚îÇ
‚îÇ 107 ‚îÇ                                                             ‚îÇ
‚îÇ 108 ‚îÇ         /// <summary>                                       ‚îÇ
‚îÇ 109 ‚îÇ         /// Handle jumping input                            ‚îÇ
‚îÇ 110 ‚îÇ         /// </summary>                                      ‚îÇ
‚îÇ 111 ‚îÇ         private void HandleJumping()                        ‚îÇ
‚îÇ 112 ‚îÇ         {                                                   ‚îÇ
‚îÇ 113 ‚îÇ             if (Input.GetKeyDown(GameConfig.Instance.jumpKey) && isGrounded) ‚îÇ
‚îÇ 114 ‚îÇ             {                                               ‚îÇ
‚îÇ 115 ‚îÇ                 velocity.y = Mathf.Sqrt(jumpHeight * -2f * gravity); ‚îÇ
‚îÇ 116 ‚îÇ                 Debug.Log("Player jumped!");                ‚îÇ
‚îÇ 117 ‚îÇ             }                                               ‚îÇ
‚îÇ 118 ‚îÇ                                                             ‚îÇ
‚îÇ 119 ‚îÇ             // Apply gravity                                ‚îÇ
‚îÇ 120 ‚îÇ             velocity.y += gravity * Time.deltaTime;         ‚îÇ
‚îÇ 121 ‚îÇ             controller.Move(velocity * Time.deltaTime);     ‚îÇ
‚îÇ 122 ‚îÇ         }                                                   ‚îÇ
‚îÇ 123 ‚îÇ                                                             ‚îÇ
‚îÇ 124 ‚îÇ         /// <summary>                                       ‚îÇ
‚îÇ 125 ‚îÇ         /// Handle interaction input                        ‚îÇ
‚îÇ 126 ‚îÇ         /// </summary>                                      ‚îÇ
‚îÇ 127 ‚îÇ         private void HandleInteraction()                    ‚îÇ
‚îÇ 128 ‚îÇ         {                                                   ‚îÇ
‚îÇ 129 ‚îÇ             if (Input.GetKeyDown(GameConfig.Instance.interactKey)) ‚îÇ
‚îÇ 130 ‚îÇ             {                                               ‚îÇ
‚îÇ 131 ‚îÇ                 // Raycast to find interactable objects     ‚îÇ
‚îÇ 132 ‚îÇ                 Ray ray = new Ray(cameraTransform.position, cameraTransform.forward); ‚îÇ
‚îÇ 133 ‚îÇ                 if (Physics.Raycast(ray, out RaycastHit hit, 3f)) ‚îÇ
‚îÇ 134 ‚îÇ                 {                                           ‚îÇ
‚îÇ 135 ‚îÇ                     // Try to interact with the object      ‚îÇ
‚îÇ 136 ‚îÇ                     var interactable = hit.collider.GetComponent<IInteractable>(); ‚îÇ
‚îÇ 137 ‚îÇ                     if (interactable != null)               ‚îÇ
‚îÇ 138 ‚îÇ                     {                                       ‚îÇ
‚îÇ 139 ‚îÇ                         interactable.Interact(this);        ‚îÇ
‚îÇ 140 ‚îÇ                         Debug.Log($"Interacted with {hit.collider.name}"); ‚îÇ
‚îÇ 141 ‚îÇ                     }                                       ‚îÇ
‚îÇ 142 ‚îÇ                 }                                           ‚îÇ
‚îÇ 143 ‚îÇ             }                                               ‚îÇ
‚îÇ 144 ‚îÇ         }                                                   ‚îÇ
‚îÇ 145 ‚îÇ                                                             ‚îÇ
‚îÇ 146 ‚îÇ         private void OnDrawGizmosSelected()                 ‚îÇ
‚îÇ 147 ‚îÇ         {                                                   ‚îÇ
‚îÇ 148 ‚îÇ             // Draw ground check sphere                     ‚îÇ

‚îÇ 156 ‚îÇ     }                                                       ‚îÇ
‚îÇ 157 ‚îÇ                                                             ‚îÇ

‚îÇ 125 ‚îÇ         /// </summary>                           ‚îÇ
‚îÇ 126 ‚îÇ         public void LogLLMInteraction(string npcName, string prompt, string response) ‚îÇ
‚îÇ 127 ‚îÇ         {                                        ‚îÇ
‚îÇ 128 ‚îÇ             if (GameConfig.Instance.enableLLMLogging) ‚îÇ
‚îÇ 129 ‚îÇ             {                                    ‚îÇ
‚îÇ 130 ‚îÇ                 LogMessage(LogLevel.LLM, "LLMChat", $"NPC: {npcName}"); ‚îÇ
‚îÇ 131 ‚îÇ                 LogMessage(LogLevel.LLM, "LLMPrompt", prompt); ‚îÇ
‚îÇ 132 ‚îÇ                 LogMessage(LogLevel.LLM, "LLMResponse", response); ‚îÇ
‚îÇ 133 ‚îÇ             }                                    ‚îÇ
‚îÇ 134 ‚îÇ         }                                        ‚îÇ
‚îÇ 135 ‚îÇ                                                  ‚îÇ
‚îÇ 136 ‚îÇ         /// <summary>                            ‚îÇ
‚îÇ 137 ‚îÇ         /// Log expansion possibilities for creative development ‚îÇ
‚îÇ 138 ‚îÇ         /// </summary>                           ‚îÇ
‚îÇ 139 ‚îÇ         public void LogExpansionIdea(string area, string idea) ‚îÇ
‚îÇ 140 ‚îÇ         {                                        ‚îÇ
‚îÇ 141 ‚îÇ             LogMessage(LogLevel.Development, "ExpansionIdea", $"[{area}] {idea}"); ‚îÇ
‚îÇ 142 ‚îÇ         }                                        ‚îÇ
‚îÇ 143 ‚îÇ                                                  ‚îÇ
‚îÇ 144 ‚îÇ         /// <summary>                            ‚îÇ
‚îÇ 145 ‚îÇ         /// Log recording information for past behavior analysis ‚îÇ
‚îÇ 146 ‚îÇ         /// </summary>                           ‚îÇ
‚îÇ 147 ‚îÇ         public void LogRecording(string behaviorType, string directory) ‚îÇ
‚îÇ 148 ‚îÇ         {                                        ‚îÇ
‚îÇ 149 ‚îÇ             LogMessage(LogLevel.Development, "Recording", $"Past {behaviorType} recordings available in: {directory}"); ‚îÇ
‚îÇ 150 ‚îÇ         }                                        ‚îÇ
‚îÇ 151 ‚îÇ                                                  ‚îÇ
‚îÇ 152 ‚îÇ         /// <summary>                            ‚îÇ
‚îÇ 153 ‚îÇ         /// Clean up old log files to prevent disk space issues ‚îÇ
‚îÇ 154 ‚îÇ         /// </summary>                           ‚îÇ
‚îÇ 155 ‚îÇ         private void CleanupOldLogs(string logDirectory) ‚îÇ
‚îÇ 156 ‚îÇ         {                                        ‚îÇ
‚îÇ 157 ‚îÇ             try                                  ‚îÇ
‚îÇ 158 ‚îÇ             {                                    ‚îÇ
‚îÇ 159 ‚îÇ                 var logFiles = Directory.GetFiles(logDirectory, "game_log_*.txt"); ‚îÇ
‚îÇ 160 ‚îÇ                 Array.Sort(logFiles);            ‚îÇ
‚îÇ 161 ‚îÇ                                                  ‚îÇ
‚îÇ 162 ‚îÇ                 if (logFiles.Length > maxLogFiles) ‚îÇ
‚îÇ 163 ‚îÇ                 {                                ‚îÇ
‚îÇ 164 ‚îÇ                     for (int i = 0; i < logFiles.Length - maxLogFiles; i++) ‚îÇ
‚îÇ 165 ‚îÇ                     {                            ‚îÇ
‚îÇ 166 ‚îÇ                         File.Delete(logFiles[i]); ‚îÇ
‚îÇ 167 ‚îÇ                         LogMessage(LogLevel.Info, "DebugLogger", $"Cleaned up old log file: {Path.GetFileName(logFiles[i])}"); ‚îÇ
‚îÇ 168 ‚îÇ                     }                            ‚îÇ
‚îÇ 169 ‚îÇ                 }                                ‚îÇ
‚îÇ 170 ‚îÇ             }                                    ‚îÇ
‚îÇ 171 ‚îÇ             catch (Exception e)                  ‚îÇ
‚îÇ 172 ‚îÇ             {                                    ‚îÇ
‚îÇ 173 ‚îÇ                 LogMessage(LogLevel.Warning, "DebugLogger", $"Failed to cleanup old logs: {e.Message}"); ‚îÇ
‚îÇ 174 ‚îÇ             }                                    ‚îÇ
‚îÇ 175 ‚îÇ         }                                        ‚îÇ
‚îÇ 176 ‚îÇ                                                  ‚îÇ
‚îÇ 177 ‚îÇ         private void OnDestroy()                 ‚îÇ
‚îÇ 178 ‚îÇ         {                                        ‚îÇ
‚îÇ 179 ‚îÇ             if (logWriter != null)               ‚îÇ
‚îÇ 180 ‚îÇ             {                                    ‚îÇ
‚îÇ 181 ‚îÇ                 LogMessage(LogLevel.Info, "DebugLogger", "Debug logging system shutting down"); ‚îÇ
‚îÇ 182 ‚îÇ                 logWriter.Close();               ‚îÇ
‚îÇ 183 ‚îÇ                 logWriter = null;                ‚îÇ
‚îÇ 184 ‚îÇ             }                                    ‚îÇ
‚îÇ 185 ‚îÇ         }                                        ‚îÇ
‚îÇ 186 ‚îÇ                                                  ‚îÇ
‚îÇ 187 ‚îÇ         private void OnApplicationPause(bool pauseStatus) ‚îÇ
‚îÇ 188 ‚îÇ         {                                        ‚îÇ
‚îÇ 189 ‚îÇ             if (pauseStatus && logWriter != null) ‚îÇ
‚îÇ 190 ‚îÇ             {                                    ‚îÇ
‚îÇ 191 ‚îÇ                 logWriter.Flush();               ‚îÇ
‚îÇ 192 ‚îÇ             }                                    ‚îÇ
‚îÇ 193 ‚îÇ         }                                        ‚îÇ
‚îÇ 194 ‚îÇ     }                                            ‚îÇ
‚îÇ 195 ‚îÇ                                                  ‚îÇ
‚îÇ 196 ‚îÇ     /// <summary>                                ‚îÇ
‚îÇ 197 ‚îÇ     /// Log level enumeration for categorizing messages ‚îÇ
‚îÇ 198 ‚îÇ     /// </summary>                               ‚îÇ
‚îÇ 199 ‚îÇ     public enum LogLevel                         ‚îÇ
‚îÇ 200 ‚îÇ     {                                            ‚îÇ
‚îÇ 201 ‚îÇ         Info,                                    ‚îÇ
‚îÇ 202 ‚îÇ         Warning,                                 ‚îÇ
‚îÇ 203 ‚îÇ         Error,                                   ‚îÇ
‚îÇ 204 ‚îÇ         Gameplay,                                ‚îÇ
‚îÇ 205 ‚îÇ         Player,                                  ‚îÇ
‚îÇ 206 ‚îÇ         LLM,                                     ‚îÇ
‚îÇ 207 ‚îÇ         Development                              ‚îÇ
‚îÇ 208 ‚îÇ     }                                            ‚îÇ
‚îÇ 209 ‚îÇ     // }}}                                       ‚îÇ
‚îÇ 210 ‚îÇ }                                                ‚îÇ

‚îÇ  13 ‚îÇ                                             ‚îÇ

‚îÇ  16 ‚îÇ    cd external-libraries/build-scripts      ‚îÇ
‚îÇ  17 ‚îÇ    ./check-dependencies.sh                  ‚îÇ
‚îÇ  18 ‚îÇ    ```                                      ‚îÇ
‚îÇ  19 ‚îÇ                                             ‚îÇ

‚îÇ  22 ‚îÇ    ./build-all.sh                           ‚îÇ
‚îÇ  23 ‚îÇ    ```                                      ‚îÇ

‚îÇ  29 ‚îÇ                                             ‚îÇ

‚îÇ  31 ‚îÇ    - Press Play in Unity Editor             ‚îÇ
‚îÇ  32 ‚îÇ    - Use WASD to move, mouse to look around ‚îÇ
‚îÇ  33 ‚îÇ    - Press Space to jump, E to interact     ‚îÇ
‚îÇ  34 ‚îÇ    - Press Escape for pause menu            ‚îÇ
‚îÇ  35 ‚îÇ                                             ‚îÇ

‚îÇ  55 ‚îÇ ```                                         ‚îÇ

‚îÇ  57 ‚îÇ ## Configuration                            ‚îÇ
‚îÇ  58 ‚îÇ                                             ‚îÇ
‚îÇ  59 ‚îÇ Game settings are stored in JSON format and can be modified at runtime: ‚îÇ
‚îÇ  60 ‚îÇ                                             ‚îÇ
‚îÇ  61 ‚îÇ - **Graphics**: Frame rate, quality, resolution ‚îÇ
‚îÇ  62 ‚îÇ - **Audio**: Volume levels for different categories   ‚îÇ

‚îÇ  64 ‚îÇ - **Development**: Debug modes and logging options ‚îÇ

‚îÇ  67 ‚îÇ                                             ‚îÇ

‚îÇ  72 ‚îÇ                                             ‚îÇ

‚îÇ   1 ‚îÇ # Unity Setup Guide for Preschool Ascension            ‚îÇ
‚îÇ   2 ‚îÇ                                                        ‚îÇ
‚îÇ   3 ‚îÇ ## Step-by-Step Unity Installation and Project Setup   ‚îÇ
‚îÇ   4 ‚îÇ                                                        ‚îÇ
‚îÇ   5 ‚îÇ ### 1. Install Unity Hub                               ‚îÇ
‚îÇ   6 ‚îÇ                                                        ‚îÇ
‚îÇ   7 ‚îÇ 1. **Download Unity Hub**:                             ‚îÇ
‚îÇ   8 ‚îÇ    - Visit [unity.com](https://unity.com/download)     ‚îÇ
‚îÇ   9 ‚îÇ    - Download Unity Hub for Linux                      ‚îÇ
‚îÇ  10 ‚îÇ    - Or use AppImage if preferred (as per project dependency policy) ‚îÇ
‚îÇ  11 ‚îÇ                                                        ‚îÇ
‚îÇ  12 ‚îÇ 2. **Install Unity Hub**:                              ‚îÇ
‚îÇ  13 ‚îÇ    ```bash                                             ‚îÇ
‚îÇ  14 ‚îÇ    # For AppImage                                      ‚îÇ
‚îÇ  15 ‚îÇ    chmod +x UnityHub.AppImage                          ‚îÇ
‚îÇ  16 ‚îÇ    ./UnityHub.AppImage                                 ‚îÇ
‚îÇ  17 ‚îÇ                                                        ‚îÇ
‚îÇ  18 ‚îÇ    # Or follow the platform-specific installation      ‚îÇ

‚îÇ  35 ‚îÇ             Type eventType = typeof(T);       ‚îÇ
‚îÇ  36 ‚îÇ                                               ‚îÇ

‚îÇ  50 ‚îÇ             Type eventType = typeof(T);       ‚îÇ
‚îÇ  51 ‚îÇ                                               ‚îÇ

‚îÇ  53 ‚îÇ             {                                 ‚îÇ

‚îÇ  55 ‚îÇ                                               ‚îÇ

‚îÇ  67 ‚îÇ         {                                     ‚îÇ
‚îÇ  68 ‚îÇ             Type eventType = typeof(T);       ‚îÇ
‚îÇ  69 ‚îÇ                                               ‚îÇ

‚îÇ  71 ‚îÇ             {                                 ‚îÇ

‚îÇ  73 ‚îÇ                                               ‚îÇ

‚îÇ  76 ‚îÇ                     try                       ‚îÇ
‚îÇ  77 ‚îÇ                     {                         ‚îÇ

‚îÇ  79 ‚îÇ                         {                     ‚îÇ
‚îÇ  80 ‚îÇ                             typedHandler.Handle(gameEvent); ‚îÇ
‚îÇ  81 ‚îÇ                         }                     ‚îÇ

‚îÇ  88 ‚îÇ             }                                 ‚îÇ

‚îÇ  16 ‚îÇ                                                      ‚îÇ

‚îÇ  19 ‚îÇ                                                      ‚îÇ
‚îÇ  20 ‚îÇ         public static ResourceManager Instance { get; private set; } ‚îÇ

‚îÇ  24 ‚îÇ             if (Instance == null)                    ‚îÇ

‚îÇ  26 ‚îÇ                 Instance = this;                     ‚îÇ
‚îÇ  27 ‚îÇ                 DontDestroyOnLoad(gameObject);       ‚îÇ
‚îÇ  28 ‚îÇ                                                      ‚îÇ
‚îÇ  29 ‚îÇ                 if (preloadCriticalResources)        ‚îÇ
‚îÇ  30 ‚îÇ                 {                                    ‚îÇ

‚îÇ  32 ‚îÇ                 }                                    ‚îÇ
‚îÇ  33 ‚îÇ             }                                        ‚îÇ

‚îÇ  35 ‚îÇ             {                                        ‚îÇ
‚îÇ  36 ‚îÇ                 Destroy(gameObject);                 ‚îÇ
‚îÇ  37 ‚îÇ             }                                        ‚îÇ
‚îÇ  38 ‚îÇ         }                                            ‚îÇ
‚îÇ  39 ‚îÇ                                                      ‚îÇ
‚îÇ  40 ‚îÇ         /// <summary>                                ‚îÇ
‚îÇ  41 ‚îÇ         /// Load a resource by path with caching     ‚îÇ
‚îÇ  42 ‚îÇ         /// </summary>                               ‚îÇ
‚îÇ  43 ‚îÇ         public T LoadResource<T>(string path) where T : UnityEngine.Object ‚îÇ
‚îÇ  44 ‚îÇ         {                                            ‚îÇ
‚îÇ  45 ‚îÇ             // Check cache first                     ‚îÇ
‚îÇ  46 ‚îÇ             if (resourceCache.ContainsKey(path))     ‚îÇ
‚îÇ  47 ‚îÇ             {                                        ‚îÇ
‚îÇ  48 ‚îÇ                 return resourceCache[path] as T;     ‚îÇ
‚îÇ  49 ‚îÇ             }                                        ‚îÇ
‚îÇ  50 ‚îÇ                                                      ‚îÇ
‚îÇ  51 ‚îÇ             // Load from Resources folder            ‚îÇ
‚îÇ  52 ‚îÇ             T resource = Resources.Load<T>(path);    ‚îÇ
‚îÇ  53 ‚îÇ                                                      ‚îÇ
‚îÇ  54 ‚îÇ             if (resource != null)                    ‚îÇ
‚îÇ  55 ‚îÇ             {                                        ‚îÇ
‚îÇ  56 ‚îÇ                 CacheResource(path, resource);       ‚îÇ
‚îÇ  57 ‚îÇ                                                      ‚îÇ
‚îÇ  58 ‚îÇ                 DebugLogger.Instance?.LogMessage(LogLevel.Info, "ResourceManager",  ‚îÇ
‚îÇ  59 ‚îÇ                     $"Loaded resource: {path} ({typeof(T).Name})"); ‚îÇ
‚îÇ  60 ‚îÇ             }                                        ‚îÇ
‚îÇ  61 ‚îÇ             else                                     ‚îÇ
‚îÇ  62 ‚îÇ             {                                        ‚îÇ
‚îÇ  63 ‚îÇ                 DebugLogger.Instance?.LogMessage(LogLevel.Warning, "ResourceManager",  ‚îÇ
‚îÇ  64 ‚îÇ                     $"Failed to load resource: {path}"); ‚îÇ
‚îÇ  65 ‚îÇ             }                                        ‚îÇ
‚îÇ  66 ‚îÇ                                                      ‚îÇ
‚îÇ  67 ‚îÇ             return resource;                         ‚îÇ
‚îÇ  68 ‚îÇ         }                                            ‚îÇ
‚îÇ  69 ‚îÇ                                                      ‚îÇ
‚îÇ  70 ‚îÇ         /// <summary>                                ‚îÇ
‚îÇ  71 ‚îÇ         /// Load all resources of a specific type    ‚îÇ
‚îÇ  72 ‚îÇ         /// </summary>                               ‚îÇ
‚îÇ  73 ‚îÇ         public T[] LoadAllResources<T>(string folder = "") where T : UnityEngine.Object ‚îÇ
‚îÇ  74 ‚îÇ         {                                            ‚îÇ
‚îÇ  75 ‚îÇ             T[] resources = Resources.LoadAll<T>(folder); ‚îÇ
‚îÇ  76 ‚îÇ                                                      ‚îÇ
‚îÇ  77 ‚îÇ             foreach (var resource in resources)      ‚îÇ
‚îÇ  78 ‚îÇ             {                                        ‚îÇ
‚îÇ  79 ‚îÇ                 string path = folder + "/" + resource.name; ‚îÇ
‚îÇ  80 ‚îÇ                 CacheResource(path, resource);       ‚îÇ
‚îÇ  81 ‚îÇ             }                                        ‚îÇ
‚îÇ  82 ‚îÇ                                                      ‚îÇ
‚îÇ  83 ‚îÇ             // Update type cache                     ‚îÇ
‚îÇ  84 ‚îÇ             Type resourceType = typeof(T);           ‚îÇ
‚îÇ  85 ‚îÇ             if (!typeCache.ContainsKey(resourceType)) ‚îÇ
‚îÇ  86 ‚îÇ             {                                        ‚îÇ
‚îÇ  87 ‚îÇ                 typeCache[resourceType] = new List<UnityEngine.Object>(); ‚îÇ
‚îÇ  88 ‚îÇ             }                                        ‚îÇ
‚îÇ  89 ‚îÇ                                                      ‚îÇ
‚îÇ  90 ‚îÇ             typeCache[resourceType].AddRange(resources); ‚îÇ
‚îÇ  91 ‚îÇ                                                      ‚îÇ
‚îÇ  92 ‚îÇ             DebugLogger.Instance?.LogMessage(LogLevel.Info, "ResourceManager",  ‚îÇ
‚îÇ  93 ‚îÇ                 $"Loaded {resources.Length} resources of type {typeof(T).Name}"); ‚îÇ
‚îÇ  94 ‚îÇ                                                      ‚îÇ
‚îÇ  95 ‚îÇ             return resources;                        ‚îÇ
‚îÇ  96 ‚îÇ         }                                            ‚îÇ
‚îÇ  97 ‚îÇ                                                      ‚îÇ
‚îÇ  98 ‚îÇ         /// <summary>                                ‚îÇ
‚îÇ  99 ‚îÇ         /// Get cached resources of a specific type  ‚îÇ
‚îÇ 100 ‚îÇ         /// </summary>                               ‚îÇ
‚îÇ 101 ‚îÇ         public List<T> GetCachedResourcesOfType<T>() where T : UnityEngine.Object ‚îÇ
‚îÇ 102 ‚îÇ         {                                            ‚îÇ
‚îÇ 103 ‚îÇ             Type resourceType = typeof(T);           ‚îÇ
‚îÇ 104 ‚îÇ             List<T> results = new List<T>();         ‚îÇ
‚îÇ 105 ‚îÇ                                                      ‚îÇ
‚îÇ 106 ‚îÇ             if (typeCache.ContainsKey(resourceType)) ‚îÇ
‚îÇ 107 ‚îÇ             {                                        ‚îÇ
‚îÇ 108 ‚îÇ                 foreach (var resource in typeCache[resourceType]) ‚îÇ
‚îÇ 109 ‚îÇ                 {                                    ‚îÇ
‚îÇ 110 ‚îÇ                     if (resource is T typedResource) ‚îÇ
‚îÇ 111 ‚îÇ                     {                                ‚îÇ
‚îÇ 112 ‚îÇ                         results.Add(typedResource);  ‚îÇ
‚îÇ 113 ‚îÇ                     }                                ‚îÇ
‚îÇ 114 ‚îÇ                 }                                    ‚îÇ
‚îÇ 115 ‚îÇ             }                                        ‚îÇ
‚îÇ 116 ‚îÇ                                                      ‚îÇ
‚îÇ 117 ‚îÇ             return results;                          ‚îÇ
‚îÇ 118 ‚îÇ         }                                            ‚îÇ
‚îÇ 119 ‚îÇ                                                      ‚îÇ
‚îÇ 120 ‚îÇ         /// <summary>                                ‚îÇ
‚îÇ 121 ‚îÇ         /// Preload critical resources for smooth gameplay ‚îÇ
‚îÇ 122 ‚îÇ         /// </summary>                               ‚îÇ
‚îÇ 123 ‚îÇ         private void PreloadCriticalResources()      ‚îÇ
‚îÇ 124 ‚îÇ         {                                            ‚îÇ
‚îÇ 125 ‚îÇ             try                                      ‚îÇ
‚îÇ 126 ‚îÇ             {                                        ‚îÇ
‚îÇ 127 ‚îÇ                 // Load configuration files          ‚îÇ
‚îÇ 128 ‚îÇ                 LoadResource<TextAsset>("default_config"); ‚îÇ
‚îÇ 129 ‚îÇ                                                      ‚îÇ
‚îÇ 130 ‚îÇ                 // Load common UI elements           ‚îÇ
‚îÇ 131 ‚îÇ                 LoadAllResources<Sprite>("UI");      ‚îÇ
‚îÇ 132 ‚îÇ                                                      ‚îÇ
‚îÇ 133 ‚îÇ                 // Load audio clips                  ‚îÇ
‚îÇ 134 ‚îÇ                 LoadAllResources<AudioClip>("Audio"); ‚îÇ
‚îÇ 135 ‚îÇ                                                      ‚îÇ
‚îÇ 136 ‚îÇ                 DebugLogger.Instance?.LogMessage(LogLevel.Info, "ResourceManager",  ‚îÇ
‚îÇ 137 ‚îÇ                     "Critical resources preloaded successfully"); ‚îÇ
‚îÇ 138 ‚îÇ             }                                        ‚îÇ
‚îÇ 139 ‚îÇ             catch (Exception e)                      ‚îÇ
‚îÇ 140 ‚îÇ             {                                        ‚îÇ
‚îÇ 141 ‚îÇ                 DebugLogger.Instance?.LogMessage(LogLevel.Error, "ResourceManager",  ‚îÇ
‚îÇ 142 ‚îÇ                     $"Error preloading critical resources: {e.Message}"); ‚îÇ
‚îÇ 143 ‚îÇ             }                                        ‚îÇ
‚îÇ 144 ‚îÇ         }                                            ‚îÇ
‚îÇ 145 ‚îÇ                                                      ‚îÇ
‚îÇ 146 ‚îÇ         /// <summary>                                ‚îÇ
‚îÇ 147 ‚îÇ         /// Cache a resource with memory management  ‚îÇ
‚îÇ 148 ‚îÇ         /// </summary>                               ‚îÇ
‚îÇ 149 ‚îÇ         private void CacheResource(string path, UnityEngine.Object resource) ‚îÇ
‚îÇ 150 ‚îÇ         {                                            ‚îÇ
‚îÇ 151 ‚îÇ             if (resourceCache.Count >= maxCachedResources) ‚îÇ
‚îÇ 152 ‚îÇ             {                                        ‚îÇ
‚îÇ 153 ‚îÇ                 // Simple LRU - remove oldest entries ‚îÇ
‚îÇ 154 ‚îÇ                 var oldestKey = "";                  ‚îÇ
‚îÇ 155 ‚îÇ                 foreach (var key in resourceCache.Keys) ‚îÇ
‚îÇ 156 ‚îÇ                 {                                    ‚îÇ
‚îÇ 157 ‚îÇ                     oldestKey = key;                 ‚îÇ
‚îÇ 158 ‚îÇ                     break;                           ‚îÇ
‚îÇ 159 ‚îÇ                 }                                    ‚îÇ
‚îÇ 160 ‚îÇ                                                      ‚îÇ
‚îÇ 161 ‚îÇ                 resourceCache.Remove(oldestKey);     ‚îÇ
‚îÇ 162 ‚îÇ             }                                        ‚îÇ
‚îÇ 163 ‚îÇ                                                      ‚îÇ
‚îÇ 164 ‚îÇ             resourceCache[path] = resource;          ‚îÇ
‚îÇ 165 ‚îÇ         }                                            ‚îÇ
‚îÇ 166 ‚îÇ                                                      ‚îÇ
‚îÇ 167 ‚îÇ         /// <summary>                                ‚îÇ
‚îÇ 168 ‚îÇ         /// Clear cached resources to free memory    ‚îÇ
‚îÇ 169 ‚îÇ         /// </summary>                               ‚îÇ
‚îÇ 170 ‚îÇ         public void ClearCache()                     ‚îÇ
‚îÇ 171 ‚îÇ         {                                            ‚îÇ
‚îÇ 172 ‚îÇ             resourceCache.Clear();                   ‚îÇ
‚îÇ 173 ‚îÇ             typeCache.Clear();                       ‚îÇ
‚îÇ 174 ‚îÇ                                                      ‚îÇ
‚îÇ 175 ‚îÇ             // Force garbage collection              ‚îÇ
‚îÇ 176 ‚îÇ             Resources.UnloadUnusedAssets();          ‚îÇ
‚îÇ 177 ‚îÇ             System.GC.Collect();                     ‚îÇ
‚îÇ 178 ‚îÇ                                                      ‚îÇ
‚îÇ 179 ‚îÇ             DebugLogger.Instance?.LogMessage(LogLevel.Info, "ResourceManager",  ‚îÇ
‚îÇ 180 ‚îÇ                 "Resource cache cleared");           ‚îÇ
‚îÇ 181 ‚îÇ         }                                            ‚îÇ
‚îÇ 182 ‚îÇ                                                      ‚îÇ
‚îÇ 183 ‚îÇ         /// <summary>                                ‚îÇ
‚îÇ 184 ‚îÇ         /// Get cache statistics for debugging       ‚îÇ
‚îÇ 185 ‚îÇ         /// </summary>                               ‚îÇ
‚îÇ 186 ‚îÇ         public void LogCacheStats()                  ‚îÇ
